+ set -e
+ type=iozone
+ bsizes='1k 4k 64k 256k 1m'
+ ops='randwrite write'
+ osync='s a'
+ three_times='1 2 3'
+ for bsize in '$bsizes'
+ for op in '$ops'
+ for sync in '$osync'
+ for xxx in '$three_times'
+ [[ s == \s ]]
+ ssync=-s
+ factor=x500
+ io_opts='--type iozone -a randwrite --iodepth 16 --blocksize 1k --iosize x500 -s'
